### [218] [Understanding and Finding JIT Compiler Performance Bugs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06551)
*Zijian Yi,Cheng Ding,August Shi,Milos Gligoric*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 首次系统研究JIT编译器性能缺陷，提出分层差分性能测试方法Jittery，在HotSpot和Graal中发现12个新性能缺陷


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JIT编译器是Java、JavaScript等语言的关键组件，现有工作主要关注功能缺陷检测，但缺乏对性能缺陷的研究。性能缺陷会导致运行时显著性能下降，且由于JIT编译器的复杂性和动态性，检测难度大。

Method: 1) 对4个主流Java和JavaScript JIT编译器进行实证研究，手动分析191个缺陷报告；2) 基于研究洞察提出分层差分性能测试技术，实现工具Jittery，包含测试优先级排序（减少92.40%测试时间）和自动过滤误报/重复等优化。

Result: 1) 揭示了JIT性能缺陷的常见触发因素、表现模式和根本原因；2) Jittery在Oracle HotSpot和Graal JIT编译器中发现了12个先前未知的性能缺陷，其中11个被确认，6个已被开发者修复。

Conclusion: 这是首个系统研究JIT编译器性能缺陷的工作，提出的分层差分性能测试方法有效，Jittery工具能够自动检测JIT性能缺陷，显著减少测试时间和人工检查工作量。

Abstract: Just-in-time (JIT) compilers are key components for many popular programming languages with managed runtimes (e.g., Java and JavaScript). JIT compilers perform optimizations and generate native code at runtime based on dynamic profiling data, to improve the execution performance of the running application. Like other software systems, JIT compilers might have software bugs, and prior work has developed a number of automated techniques for detecting functional bugs (i.e., generated native code does not semantically match that of the original code). However, no prior work has targeted JIT compiler performance bugs, which can cause significant performance degradation while an application is running. These performance bugs are challenging to detect due to the complexity and dynamic nature of JIT compilers. In this paper, we present the first work on demystifying JIT performance bugs. First, we perform an empirical study across four popular JIT compilers for Java and JavaScript. Our manual analysis of 191 bug reports uncovers common triggers of performance bugs, patterns in which these bugs manifest, and their root causes. Second, informed by these insights, we propose layered differential performance testing, a lightweight technique to automatically detect JIT compiler performance bugs, and implement it in a tool called Jittery. We incorporate practical optimizations into Jittery such as test prioritization, which reduces testing time by 92.40% without compromising bug-detection capability, and automatic filtering of false-positives and duplicates, which substantially reduces manual inspection effort. Using Jittery, we discovered 12 previously unknown performance bugs in the Oracle HotSpot and Graal JIT compilers, with 11 confirmed and 6 fixed by developers.

</details>

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RoboLayout扩展LayoutVLM，通过集成可达性约束和局部优化，生成适合不同具身智能体交互的室内场景布局


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型在空间推理和3D场景布局生成方面有进展，但生成的布局往往缺乏对具身智能体的交互可行性考虑，特别是在物理受限的室内环境中

Method: 1. 在可微分布局优化过程中集成显式的可达性约束；2. 提出局部细化阶段，选择性重新优化有问题的物体放置；3. 支持多种具身智能体抽象（服务机器人、仓库机器人、不同年龄段人类、动物等）

Result: RoboLayout保持了LayoutVLM的语义对齐和物理合理性，同时增强了面向智能体的室内场景生成适用性，在不同场景配置下实验验证了有效性

Conclusion: RoboLayout通过智能体感知推理和改进的优化稳定性，实现了既语义连贯又适合具身智能体交互的室内场景布局生成，扩展了视觉语言模型在具身AI环境设计中的应用

Abstract: Recent advances in vision language models (VLMs) have shown strong potential for spatial reasoning and 3D scene layout generation from open-ended language instructions. However, generating layouts that are not only semantically coherent but also feasible for interaction by embodied agents remains challenging, particularly in physically constrained indoor environments. In this paper, RoboLayout is introduced as an extension of LayoutVLM that augments the original framework with agent-aware reasoning and improved optimization stability. RoboLayout integrates explicit reachability constraints into a differentiable layout optimization process, enabling the generation of layouts that are navigable and actionable by embodied agents. Importantly, the agent abstraction is not limited to a specific robot platform and can represent diverse entities with distinct physical capabilities, such as service robots, warehouse robots, humans of different age groups, or animals, allowing environment design to be tailored to the intended agent. In addition, a local refinement stage is proposed that selectively reoptimizes problematic object placements while keeping the remainder of the scene fixed, improving convergence efficiency without increasing global optimization iterations. Overall, RoboLayout preserves the strong semantic alignment and physical plausibility of LayoutVLM while enhancing applicability to agent-centric indoor scene generation, as demonstrated by experimental results across diverse scene configurations.

### [220] [Real-Time AI Service Economy: A Framework for Agentic Computing Across the Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05614)
*Lauri Lovén,Alaa Saleh,Reza Farahani,Ilir Murturi,Miguel Bordallo López,Praveen Kumar Donta,Schahram Dustdar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文研究了在设备-边缘-云连续体中，服务依赖图（DAG）的拓扑结构如何影响去中心化价格资源分配的稳定性，发现层次化结构（树状或串并联）能实现稳定均衡，而复杂交叉依赖会导致价格振荡；提出混合管理架构来封装复杂子图为资源切片，显著降低价格波动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实时AI服务在设备-边缘-云连续体中运行时，自主AI代理生成延迟敏感的工作负载，编排多阶段处理管道，并在策略和治理约束下竞争共享资源。需要理解去中心化、基于价格的资源分配在何种条件下能够可靠地大规模工作。

Method: 将服务依赖建模为DAG（有向无环图），节点表示计算阶段，边编码执行顺序。分析不同拓扑结构（层次化vs复杂交叉依赖）对价格稳定性的影响。提出混合管理架构，其中跨域集成器将复杂子图封装为资源切片，向市场呈现更简单、结构良好的接口。通过系统消融研究（6个实验，1,620次运行，每个10个种子）验证。

Result: 1) 依赖图拓扑是价格稳定性和可扩展性的首要决定因素；2) 混合架构将价格波动降低70-75%而不牺牲吞吐量；3) 治理约束产生可量化的效率-合规权衡，取决于拓扑和负载；4) 在真实出价下，去中心化市场匹配集中化价值最优基线。

Conclusion: 服务依赖图的拓扑结构是去中心化资源分配能否可靠工作的关键。层次化结构支持稳定均衡和高效计算，而复杂交叉依赖需要混合架构来封装复杂性。去中心化协调在适当条件下可以复制集中化分配质量，为跨设备-边缘-云连续体的实时AI服务提供可行的管理方案。

Abstract: Real-time AI services increasingly operate across the device-edge-cloud continuum, where autonomous AI agents generate latency-sensitive workloads, orchestrate multi-stage processing pipelines, and compete for shared resources under policy and governance constraints. This article shows that the structure of service-dependency graphs, modelled as DAGs whose nodes represent compute stages and whose edges encode execution ordering, is a primary determinant of whether decentralised, price-based resource allocation can work reliably at scale. When dependency graphs are hierarchical (tree or series-parallel), prices converge to stable equilibria, optimal allocations can be computed efficiently, and under appropriate mechanism design (with quasilinear utilities and discrete slice items), agents have no incentive to misreport their valuations within each decision epoch. When dependencies are more complex, with cross-cutting ties between pipeline stages, prices oscillate, allocation quality degrades, and the system becomes difficult to manage. To bridge this gap, we propose a hybrid management architecture in which cross-domain integrators encapsulate complex sub-graphs into resource slices that present a simpler, well-structured interface to the rest of the market. A systematic ablation study across six experiments (1,620 runs, 10 seeds each) confirms that (i) dependency-graph topology is a first-order determinant of price stability and scalability,(ii) the hybrid architecture reduces price volatility by up to 70-75% without sacrificing throughput, (iii) governance constraints create quantifiable efficiency-compliance trade-offs that depend jointly on topology and load, and (iv) under truthful bidding the decentralised market matches a centralised value-optimal baseline, confirming that decentralised coordination can replicate centralised allocation quality.

</details>


### [221] [Reasoning Models Struggle to Control their Chains of Thought](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05706)
*Chen Yueh-Han,Robert McCarthy,Bruce W. Lee,He He,Ian Kivlichan,Bowen Baker,Micah Carroll,Tomek Korbak*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究评估大语言模型的思维链可控性，发现模型难以控制思维链内容，这对思维链监控是积极信号


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 思维链监控是检测模型不当行为的重要工具，但如果模型能控制思维链内容，会破坏监控有效性。需要评估这种"思维链可控性"风险

Method: 提出CoT-Control评估套件，测试模型在遵循特定思维链指令（如不使用特定词汇）时解决问题的能力。比较不同模型、训练方式、计算资源和任务难度下的表现

Result: 模型思维链可控性显著低于最终输出可控性（Claude Sonnet 4.5仅2.7% vs 61.9%）。可控性随模型增大而提高，但随RL训练、测试计算和问题难度增加而降低。对抗性提示优化无法显著提高可控性

Conclusion: 目前思维链可控性不太可能成为监控失效的原因，但机制尚不明确。建议前沿实验室在未来模型中持续跟踪思维链可控性

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring is a promising tool for detecting misbehaviors and understanding the motivations of modern reasoning models. However, if models can control what they verbalize in their CoT, it could undermine CoT monitorability. To measure this undesirable capability -- CoT controllability -- we introduce the CoT-Control evaluation suite, which includes tasks that require models to solve problems while adhering to CoT instructions, e.g., reasoning about a genetics question without using the word 'chromosome'. We show that reasoning models possess significantly lower CoT controllability than output controllability; for instance, Claude Sonnet 4.5 can control its CoT only 2.7% of the time but 61.9% when controlling its final output. We also find that CoT controllability is higher for larger models and decreases with more RL training, test-time compute, and increased problem difficulty. CoT controllability failures extend even to situations in which models are given incentives (as opposed to direct requests) to evade CoT monitors, although models exhibit slightly higher controllability when they are told they are being monitored. Similarly, eliciting controllability by adversarially optimizing prompts does not meaningfully increase controllability. Our results leave us cautiously optimistic that CoT controllability is currently unlikely to be a failure mode of CoT monitorability. However, the mechanism behind low controllability is not well understood. Given its importance for maintaining CoT monitorability, we recommend that frontier labs track CoT controllability in future models.

</details>


### [222] [Evolving Medical Imaging Agents via Experience-driven Self-skill Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05860)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MACRO从已验证的执行轨迹中自主识别重复出现的有效多步骤工具序列，将其合成为可复用的复合工具，并注册为新的高级原语。采用轻量级图像特征记忆将工具选择基于视觉-临床上下文，通过GRPO-like训练循环强化发现的复合工具的可靠调用，实现闭环自改进。

Abstract: Clinical image interpretation is inherently multi-step and tool-centric: clinicians iteratively combine visual evidence with patient context, quantify findings, and refine their decisions through a sequence of specialized procedures. While LLM-based agents promise to orchestrate such heterogeneous medical tools, existing systems treat tool sets and invocation strategies as static after deployment. This design is brittle under real-world domain shifts, across tasks, and evolving diagnostic requirements, where predefined tool chains frequently degrade and demand costly manual re-design. We propose MACRO, a self-evolving, experience-augmented medical agent that shifts from static tool composition to experience-driven tool discovery. From verified execution trajectories, the agent autonomously identifies recurring effective multi-step tool sequences, synthesizes them into reusable composite tools, and registers these as new high-level primitives that continuously expand its behavioral repertoire. A lightweight image-feature memory grounds tool selection in a visual-clinical context, while a GRPO-like training loop reinforces reliable invocation of discovered composites, enabling closed-loop self-improvement with minimal supervision. Extensive experiments across diverse medical imaging datasets and tasks demonstrate that autonomous composite tool discovery consistently improves multi-step orchestration accuracy and cross-domain generalization over strong baselines and recent state-of-the-art agentic methods, bridging the gap between brittle static tool use and adaptive, context-aware clinical AI assistance. Code will be available upon acceptance.

### [223] [The World Won't Stay Still: Programmable Evolution for Agent Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05910)
*Guangrui Li,Yaochen Xie,Yi Liu,Ziwei Dong,Xingyuan Pan,Tianqi Zheng,Jason Choi,Michael J. Morais,Binit Jha,Shaunak Mishra,Bingrou Zhou,Chen Luo,Monica Xiao Cheng,Dawn Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ProEvolve：基于图的可编程环境演化框架，用于评估LLM智能体在动态环境中的适应性

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试大多假设静态环境，忽略了现实世界的演化特性和智能体对环境变化的鲁棒性评估需求

Method: 提出基于类型化关系图的统一环境表示框架，通过图变换实现环境演化编程，支持自动生成环境和任务沙箱

Result: 成功将单一环境演化为200个环境和3000个任务沙箱，并基于此对代表性智能体进行了基准测试

Conclusion: ProEvolve为评估LLM智能体在动态环境中的适应性提供了可扩展、可控的解决方案

Abstract: LLM-powered agents fulfill user requests by interacting with environments, querying data, and invoking tools in a multi-turn process. Yet, most existing benchmarks assume static environments with fixed schemas and toolsets, neglecting the evolutionary nature of the real world and agents' robustness to environmental changes. In this paper, we study a crucial problem: how to evolve the agent environment in a scalable and controllable way, thereby better evaluating agents' adaptability to real-world dynamics. We propose ProEvolve, a graph-based framework that makes environment evolution programmable. At its core, a typed relational graph provides a unified, explicit representation of the environment: data, tools, and schema. Under this formalism, adding, removing, or modifying capabilities are expressed as graph transformations that coherently propagate updates across tools, schemas, and data access. Building on this, ProEvolve can (1) program the evolutionary dynamics as graph transformations to generate environments automatically, and (2) instantiate task sandboxes via subgraph sampling and programming. We validate ProEvolve by evolving a single environment into 200 environments and 3,000 task sandboxes, and benchmark representative agents accordingly.

### [224] [DeepFact: Co-Evolving Benchmarks and Agents for Deep Research Factuality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05912)
*Yukun Huang,Leonardo F. R. Ribeiro,Momchil Hardalov,Bhuwan Dhingra,Markus Dreyer,Venkatesh Saligrama*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出AtS方法构建可演化的DRR事实性基准，并开发DeepFact-Bench基准和DeepFact-Eval验证代理，显著提升专家标注准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有事实核查工具主要针对通用领域的事实性原子声明，缺乏针对深度研究报告(DRR)的声明级事实性验证基准，且静态专家标注基准在此场景下脆弱不可靠。

Method: 提出Evolving Benchmarking via Audit-then-Score (AtS)方法：当验证器与当前基准不一致时，需提交证据；审计员裁决争议；接受的修订更新基准后再评估模型。基于此构建DeepFact-Bench版本化基准和DeepFact-Eval文档级验证代理。

Result: 通过四轮AtS迭代，专家微金标准确率从60.8%提升至90.9%；DeepFact-Eval在DeepFact-Bench上优于现有验证器，并在外部事实性数据集上表现良好。

Conclusion: AtS方法能有效构建可靠的DRR事实性基准，专家作为审计员比一次性标注员更可靠；DeepFact-Bench和DeepFact-Eval为DRR事实性验证提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Search-augmented LLM agents can produce deep research reports (DRRs), but verifying claim-level factuality remains challenging. Existing fact-checkers are primarily designed for general-domain, factoid-style atomic claims, and there is no benchmark to test whether such verifiers transfer to DRRs. Yet building such a benchmark is itself difficult. We first show that static expert-labeled benchmarks are brittle in this setting: in a controlled study with PhD-level specialists, unassisted experts achieve only 60.8% accuracy on a hidden micro-gold set of verifiable claims. We propose Evolving Benchmarking via Audit-then-Score (AtS), where benchmark labels and rationales are explicitly revisable: when a verifier disagrees with the current benchmark, it must submit evidence; an auditor adjudicates the dispute; and accepted revisions update the benchmark before models are scored. Across four AtS rounds, expert micro-gold accuracy rises to 90.9%, indicating experts are substantially more reliable as auditors than as one-shot labelers. We instantiate AtS as DeepFact-Bench, a versioned DRR factuality benchmark with auditable rationales, and DeepFact-Eval, a document-level verification agent (with a grouped lite variant) that outperforms existing verifiers on DeepFact-Bench and transfers well to external factuality datasets.

</details>

*Bin Xuan,Ruo Ai,Hakyeon Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出基于大语言模型的多智能体系统，用于自动化产品概念评估，通过八个虚拟专家代理进行技术可行性和市场可行性评估，其评估结果与行业专家一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 产品概念评估对企业资源分配和项目成功至关重要，但传统专家主导方法存在主观偏见、高时间和成本等问题，需要更客观高效的自动化评估方法。

Method: 1) 建立技术可行性和市场可行性两个评估维度；2) 构建包含八个虚拟代理（如研发、营销等专业领域）的多智能体系统；3) 使用检索增强生成和实时搜索工具收集客观证据；4) 基于标准进行结构化审议；5) 用专业产品评审数据微调代理以提高判断准确性。

Result: 专业显示器概念的案例研究表明，系统的评估排名与资深行业专家的评估结果一致，验证了多智能体评估方法在产品开发决策支持中的可用性。

Conclusion: 基于大语言模型的多智能体系统能够有效支持产品概念评估，提供客观、高效的自动化评估方案，可作为产品开发决策的有力工具。

Abstract: Product concept evaluation is a critical stage that determines strategic resource allocation and project success in enterprises. However, traditional expert-led approaches face limitations such as subjective bias and high time and cost requirements. To support this process, this study proposes an automated approach utilizing a large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent system (MAS). Through a systematic analysis of previous research on product development and team collaboration, this study established two primary evaluation dimensions, namely technical feasibility and market feasibility. The proposed system consists of a team of eight virtual agents representing specialized domains such as R&D and marketing. These agents use retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) and real-time search tools to gather objective evidence and validate concepts through structured deliberations based on the established criteria. The agents were further fine-tuned using professional product review data to enhance their judgment accuracy. A case study involving professional display monitor concepts demonstrated that the system's evaluation rankings were consistent with those of senior industry experts. These results confirm the usability of the proposed multi-agent-based evaluation approach for supporting product development decisions.

### [226] [Agentic LLM Planning via Step-Wise PDDL Simulation: An Empirical Characterisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06064)
*Kai Göbel,Pierrick Lorang,Patrik Zips,Tobias Glück*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出PyPDDLEngine，一个通过MCP接口将PDDL规划操作作为LLM工具调用的开源引擎，评估了四种规划方法在Blocksworld任务上的表现，发现代理式LLM规划比直接LLM规划有3%的优势，但成本更高，且LLM规划可能更多依赖训练数据回忆而非通用规划能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大型语言模型是否能够作为可行的规划器与经典符号方法相媲美，特别是在任务规划这一机器人自主系统的核心能力方面。研究代理式交互规划与直接规划的性能差异。

Method: 开发了PyPDDLEngine，一个开源的PDDL仿真引擎，通过MCP接口将规划操作暴露为LLM工具调用。LLM作为交互式搜索策略，一次选择一个动作，观察结果状态，并可重置重试。在102个IPC Blocksworld实例上评估了四种方法：Fast Downward的两种经典规划器、直接LLM规划（Claude Haiku 4.5）和通过PyPDDLEngine的代理式LLM规划。

Result: Fast Downward达到85.3%成功率。直接LLM规划63.7%，代理式LLM规划66.7%，代理式方法有3个百分点的优势，但每个解决方案的token成本高5.7倍。在大多数共同解决的难度块中，两种LLM方法产生的计划比seq-sat-lama-2011更短，尽管后者有迭代质量改进。

Conclusion: 代理式规划的收益取决于环境反馈的性质。编码代理受益于编译器错误和测试失败等外部基础信号，而PDDL步骤反馈是自我评估的，让代理在没有外部验证的情况下评估自己的进展。LLM规划可能更多依赖训练数据回忆而非通用规划能力。

Abstract: Task planning, the problem of sequencing actions to reach a goal from an initial state, is a core capability requirement for autonomous robotic systems. Whether large language models (LLMs) can serve as viable planners alongside classical symbolic methods remains an open question. We present PyPDDLEngine, an open-source Planning Domain Definition Language (PDDL) simulation engine that exposes planning operations as LLM tool calls through a Model Context Protocol (MCP) interface. Rather than committing to a complete action sequence upfront, the LLM acts as an interactive search policy that selects one action at a time, observes each resulting state, and can reset and retry. We evaluate four approaches on 102 International Planning Competition (IPC) Blocksworld instances under a uniform 180-second budget: Fast Downward lama-first and seq-sat-lama-2011 as classical baselines, direct LLM planning (Claude Haiku 4.5), and agentic LLM planning via PyPDDLEngine. Fast Downward achieves 85.3% success. The direct and agentic LLM approaches achieve 63.7% and 66.7%, respectively, a consistent but modest three-percentage-point advantage for the agentic approach at $5.7\times$ higher token cost per solution. Across most co-solved difficulty blocks, both LLM approaches produce shorter plans than seq-sat-lama-2011 despite its iterative quality improvement, a result consistent with training-data recall rather than generalisable planning. These results suggest that agentic gains depend on the nature of environmental feedback. Coding agents benefit from externally grounded signals such as compiler errors and test failures, whereas PDDL step feedback is self-assessed, leaving the agent to evaluate its own progress without external verification.

*Yann Munro,Isabelle Bloch,Marie-Jeanne Lesot*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有定量双极论证框架中的渐进语义在处理攻击者和支持者时通常采用对称方式，但实际情境中攻击者和支持者可能扮演不对称角色。需要更灵活、可参数化且易于理解的语义来适应不同情境。

Method: 提出聚合语义家族，采用三阶段计算：1) 计算攻击者的全局权重；2) 计算支持者的全局权重；3) 将这两个值与论证的固有权重聚合。讨论了三种聚合函数应满足的性质及其与传统渐进语义原则的关系。

Result: 通过简单示例和最终示例（测试比较500种聚合语义）展示了聚合语义的可能行为范围。三阶段分解使计算更具参数化，保持了双极性，并产生了更易理解的渐进语义。

Conclusion: 聚合语义为定量双极论证框架提供了一种新颖、灵活且可解释的方法，通过分离处理攻击者和支持者，增强了语义的参数化和可理解性，适用于攻击者和支持者角色不对称的实际情境。

Abstract: Formal argumentation is being used increasingly in artificial intelligence as an effective and understandable way to model potentially conflicting pieces of information, called arguments, and identify so-called acceptable arguments depending on a chosen semantics. This paper deals with the specific context of Quantitative Bipolar Argumentation Frameworks (QBAF), where arguments have intrinsic weights and can attack or support each other. In this context, we introduce a novel family of gradual semantics, called aggregative semantics. In order to deal with situations in which attackers and supporters do not play a symmetric role, and in contrast to modular semantics, we propose to aggregate attackers and supporters separately. This leads to a three-stage computation, which consists in computing a global weight for attackers and another for supporters, before aggregating these two values with the intrinsic weight of the argument. We discuss the properties that the three aggregation functions should satisfy depending on the context, as well as their relationships with the classical principles for gradual semantics. This discussion is supported by various simple examples, as well as a final example on which five hundred aggregative semantics are tested and compared, illustrating the range of possible behaviours with aggregative semantics. Decomposing the computation into three distinct and interpretable steps leads to a more parametrisable computation: it keeps the bipolarity one step further than what is done in the literature, and it leads to more understandable gradual semantics.

### [232] [SAHOO: Safeguarded Alignment for High-Order Optimization Objectives in Recursive Self-Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06333)
*Subramanyam Sahoo,Aman Chadha,Vinija Jain,Divya Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SAHOO框架通过多信号检测、约束保持和回归风险评估来监控和控制递归自我改进中的对齐漂移，在代码生成和数学推理任务中实现显著质量提升，同时保持安全约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 递归自我改进正从理论走向实践，但迭代自我修改可能导致微妙的对齐漂移风险。需要一种实用框架来监控和控制这种漂移，确保在系统自我改进过程中保持对齐性。

Method: 提出SAHOO框架，包含三个安全措施：(1) 目标漂移指数(GDI)，结合语义、词汇、结构和分布度量的多信号检测器；(2) 约束保持检查，强制执行安全关键不变性；(3) 回归风险评估，标记可能撤销先前改进的改进周期。

Result: 在189个代码生成、数学推理和真实性任务中，SAHOO实现显著质量提升：代码任务提升18.3%，推理任务提升16.8%，同时在两个领域保持约束，真实性任务中违规率较低。阈值在18个任务的验证集上校准。

Conclusion: SAHOO使递归自我改进过程中的对齐保持变得可测量、可部署和可系统验证。研究还揭示了能力-对齐前沿，显示早期改进周期效率高但后期对齐成本上升，以及领域特定的权衡（如流畅性与事实性）。

Abstract: Recursive self-improvement is moving from theory to practice: modern systems can critique, revise, and evaluate their own outputs, yet iterative self-modification risks subtle alignment drift. We introduce SAHOO, a practical framework to monitor and control drift through three safeguards: (i) the Goal Drift Index (GDI), a learned multi-signal detector combining semantic, lexical, structural, and distributional measures; (ii) constraint preservation checks that enforce safety-critical invariants such as syntactic correctness and non-hallucination; and (iii) regression-risk quantification to flag improvement cycles that undo prior gains. Across 189 tasks in code generation, mathematical reasoning, and truthfulness, SAHOO produces substantial quality gains, including 18.3 percent improvement in code tasks and 16.8 percent in reasoning, while preserving constraints in two domains and maintaining low violations in truthfulness. Thresholds are calibrated on a small validation set of 18 tasks across three cycles. We further map the capability-alignment frontier, showing efficient early improvement cycles but rising alignment costs later and exposing domain-specific tensions such as fluency versus factuality. SAHOO therefore makes alignment preservation during recursive self-improvement measurable, deployable, and systematically validated at scale.

### [233] [Talk Freely, Execute Strictly: Schema-Gated Agentic AI for Flexible and Reproducible Scientific Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06394)
*Joel Strickland,Arjun Vijeta,Chris Moores,Oliwia Bodek,Bogdan Nenchev,Thomas Whitehead,Charles Phillips,Karl Tassenberg,Gareth Conduit,Ben Pellegrini*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出schema-gated orchestration架构，通过模式验证分离对话灵活性和执行确定性，解决LLM科学工作流中的确定性与灵活性矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM能将自然语言目标转化为可执行计算，但科学工作流需要确定性、可追溯性和治理保障，而LLM自主决策难以保证这些要求。工业R&D专家访谈揭示了确定性约束执行与对话灵活性之间的冲突。

Method: 提出schema-gated orchestration原则：模式作为组合工作流级别的强制执行边界，所有操作必须通过机器可检查的规范验证。将需求操作化为执行确定性(ED)和对话灵活性(CF)，使用多模型LLM评分协议评估20个系统，验证架构评估的可靠性。

Result: 多模型LLM评分显示高度一致性（ED α=0.80，CF α=0.98），证明可作为专家评估的替代方案。现有系统存在Pareto前沿，无法同时实现高灵活性和高确定性，但在生成式和流程中心化极端之间出现收敛区域。

Conclusion: schema-gated架构通过分离对话和执行权限，能够解耦灵活性与确定性的权衡。提出三个操作原则：执行前澄清、约束的计划-执行编排、工具到工作流级别的门控，以指导实际应用。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can now translate a researcher's plain-language goal into executable computation, yet scientific workflows demand determinism, provenance, and governance that are difficult to guarantee when an LLM decides what runs. Semi-structured interviews with 18 experts across 10 industrial R&D stakeholders surface 2 competing requirements--deterministic, constrained execution and conversational flexibility without workflow rigidity--together with boundary properties (human-in-the-loop control and transparency) that any resolution must satisfy. We propose schema-gated orchestration as the resolving principle: the schema becomes a mandatory execution boundary at the composed-workflow level, so that nothing runs unless the complete action--including cross-step dependencies--validates against a machine-checkable specification.
  We operationalize the 2 requirements as execution determinism (ED) and conversational flexibility (CF), and use these axes to review 20 systems spanning 5 architectural groups along a validation-scope spectrum. Scores are assigned via a multi-model protocol--15 independent sessions across 3 LLM families--yielding substantial-to-near-perfect inter-model agreement (Krippendorff a=0.80 for ED and a=0.98 for CF), demonstrating that multi-model LLM scoring can serve as a reusable alternative to human expert panels for architectural assessment.
  The resulting landscape reveals an empirical Pareto front--no reviewed system achieves both high flexibility and high determinism--but a convergence zone emerges between the generative and workflow-centric extremes. We argue that a schema-gated architecture, separating conversational from execution authority, is positioned to decouple this trade-off, and distill 3 operational principles--clarification-before-execution, constrained plan-act orchestration, and tool-to-workflow-level gating--to guide adoption.

</details>


### [234] [Boosting deep Reinforcement Learning using pretraining with Logical Options](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06565)
*Zihan Ye,Phil Chau,Raban Emunds,Jannis Blüml,Cedric Derstroff,Quentin Delfosse,Oleg Arenz,Kristian Kersting*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出H^2RL混合分层强化学习方法，结合符号逻辑与神经网络，解决深度强化学习中的短期奖励过度利用问题，提升长期决策能力


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度强化学习智能体经常出现对齐问题，过度利用早期奖励信号。纯符号方法难以扩展到连续环境，需要结合神经网络的表达能力

Method: 提出两阶段混合框架：1) 使用基于逻辑选项的预训练策略引导学习策略远离短期奖励循环；2) 通过标准环境交互精炼最终策略，将符号结构注入神经强化学习智能体

Result: 实验证明该方法能持续改善长期决策能力，在多个任务上优于强大的神经、符号和神经符号基线方法

Conclusion: H^2RL成功将符号结构注入神经强化学习，既保持了深度策略的表达能力，又解决了对齐问题，为混合方法在连续环境中的应用提供了有效方案

Abstract: Deep reinforcement learning agents are often misaligned, as they over-exploit early reward signals. Recently, several symbolic approaches have addressed these challenges by encoding sparse objectives along with aligned plans. However, purely symbolic architectures are complex to scale and difficult to apply to continuous settings. Hence, we propose a hybrid approach, inspired by humans' ability to acquire new skills. We use a two-stage framework that injects symbolic structure into neural-based reinforcement learning agents without sacrificing the expressivity of deep policies. Our method, called Hybrid Hierarchical RL (H^2RL), introduces a logical option-based pretraining strategy to steer the learning policy away from short-term reward loops and toward goal-directed behavior while allowing the final policy to be refined via standard environment interaction. Empirically, we show that this approach consistently improves long-horizon decision-making and yields agents that outperform strong neural, symbolic, and neuro-symbolic baselines.

</details>

### [235] [From Line Knowledge Digraphs to Sheaf Semantics: A Categorical Framework for Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05685)
*Moses Boudourides*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 提出一个将知识图谱的图结构与拓扑语义学结合的分类框架，通过格罗滕迪克拓扑和层理论支持上下文相关的语义推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统知识图谱缺乏对上下文依赖语义的建模能力，需要统一的数学框架来连接图论结构、分类组合和语义推理。

Method: 将知识图谱表示为带标签的有向多重图，通过关联矩阵和线知识有向图构造分析。构建图的自由范畴，定义格罗滕迪克拓扑，生成层的拓扑，支持局部到全局的语义推理。

Result: 建立了一个统一的数学模型，将图论结构、分类组合和层语义连接起来，为上下文相关的关系推理提供了形式化基础。

Conclusion: 该分类框架为知识图谱提供了强大的语义建模能力，通过拓扑理论实现了上下文依赖的推理，为关系知识表示开辟了新方向。

Abstract: This paper proposes a categorical framework for knowledge graphs linking combinatorial graph structure with topos-theoretic semantics. Knowledge graphs are represented as labelled directed multigraphs and analysed through incidence matrices and line knowledge digraph constructions. The graph induces a free category whose morphisms correspond to relational paths. To model context-dependent meaning, a Grothendieck topology is defined on the free category generated by the graph leading to a topos of sheaves that supports local-to-global semantic reasoning. The framework connects graph-theoretic structure, categorical composition, and sheaf semantics in a unified mathematical model for contextual relational reasoning.

</details>


### [236] [The Architects of Narrative Evolution: Actor Interventions Across the SAGES Framework in Information Campaigns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05802)
*Lynnette Hui Xian Ng,Yukai Zeng,Muthiah Ponmani*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: SAGES框架扩展：五阶段叙事演化模型，分析数字空间中敌对与建设性行为者如何操纵叙事轨迹，通过缅甸政变和俄乌战争案例展示应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字空间中的叙事并非自然现象，而是被各类行为者战略性地塑造以影响公众认知、行为和社会政治结果。现有研究需要更系统的框架来分析叙事操纵活动及其应对策略。

Method: 提出SAGES框架的扩展版本，包含五个阶段：播种、放大、激发、扩展和粘性。通过缅甸2021年军事政变和2022年俄乌战争的比较案例研究，展示叙事操纵活动如何展开以及针对性干预如何减轻其影响。

Result: SAGES框架为分析影响力行动和制定对策提供了实用视角，展示了不同行为者在叙事演化的每个阶段如何干预以加速、转向或对抗叙事轨迹。

Conclusion: 该框架在信息生态系统竞争激烈的时代，为理解叙事操纵和制定有效应对措施提供了系统化的分析工具，有助于识别和缓解叙事操纵活动的影响。

Abstract: Narratives in digital spaces are not merely organic phenomena. They are strategically shaped by a range of actors to influence public perception, behavior, and sociopolitical outcomes. This paper offers an actor-oriented expansion of the SAGES Framework, a five-stage model that traces the evolution of narratives from digital inception to real-world impact: Seeding, Amplification, Galvanization, Expansion, and Stickiness. This framework maps how adversarial and constructive actors intervene at each stage to accelerate, redirect, or counter narrative trajectories. Through comparative case studies of the 2021 Myanmar military coup and the 2022 Russia-Ukraine war, we show how narrative manipulation campaigns unfold and how targeted interventions can mitigate their effects. The SAGES framework contributes a practical lens for analyzing influence operations and developing countermeasures in an era of contested information ecosystems.

</details>


### [237] [Rethinking Thematic Evolution in Science Mapping: An Integrated Framework for Longitudinal Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06436)
*Massimo Aria,Luca D'Aniello,Michelangelo Misuraca,Maria Spano*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 提出一个结构整合框架，将主题谱系重建嵌入到与横截面检测相同的加权关系架构中，通过分级文档隶属度和谱系强度度量来建模主题连续性，将演化概念化为关系结构的重构而非简单词汇持续性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有纵向科学图谱方法存在结构不一致性：主题通过加权网络中的关系聚类检测，而时间连接通常基于关键词或核心文档的集合论重叠推断。这种不一致影响了方法的一致性和解释的稳健性。

Method: 引入结构整合框架，将谱系重建嵌入到与横截面检测相同的加权关系架构中。通过分级文档隶属度和谱系强度度量（结合方向覆盖度和中心性加权的结构相关性）来建模主题连续性。

Result: 该框架将主题检测和时间建模统一在关系范式中，增强了纵向科学图谱的方法一致性和解释稳健性，将演化概念化为关系结构的重构而非简单词汇持续性。

Conclusion: 通过将主题检测和时序建模统一在关系范式中，该框架提高了纵向科学图谱的方法一致性和解释稳健性，为科学领域的概念结构演化提供了更连贯的分析方法。

Abstract: Strategic diagrams and co-word analysis are widely employed to examine the conceptual structure of scientific domains and their development over time. Yet a structural inconsistency characterises dominant longitudinal implementations: themes are detected through relational clustering in weighted networks, whereas their inter-temporal connections are commonly inferred from set-theoretic overlap among keywords or core documents. This study introduces a structurally integrated framework in which lineage reconstruction is embedded within the same weighted relational architecture that underpins cross-sectional detection. The approach models thematic continuity through graded document affiliation and a lineage-strength measure that combines directional coverage with centrality-weighted structural relevance, thereby conceptualising evolution as the reconfiguration of relational structures rather than simple lexical persistence. By aligning thematic detection and temporal modelling within a unified relational paradigm, the framework enhances the methodological coherence and interpretive robustness of longitudinal science mapping.

</details>


### [238] [Mapping the long-term trajectories of political violence in Africa](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06502)
*Steven M. Radil,Nick Dorward,Olivier Walther,Levi John Wolf*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种空间显式的纵向序列分析方法，用于研究政治暴力的长期轨迹，识别出六种从短期局部爆发到长期高强度冲突的反复模式，并揭示了边境地区的空间相互依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有政治暴力模型通常关注离散的冲突转变（如爆发、升级或平息），而忽视了暴力在时间和空间上累积的长期轨迹。这种局限性需要一种能够捕捉暴力生命周期和空间动态的新方法。

Method: 采用空间显式的纵向序列分析，使用1997-2024年非洲武装冲突地点和事件数据集的事件级数据，根据暴力强度和空间集中度对地点进行分类，应用最优匹配和聚类技术识别冲突轨迹模式。

Result: 识别出六种反复出现的冲突轨迹模式，涵盖从短期局部爆发到长期高强度冲突的连续谱系。研究发现相邻地区（特别是边境区域）存在空间相互依赖性，表明冲突轨迹在空间上相互关联。

Conclusion: 该研究通过强调政治暴力的时间节奏和地理联系，推动冲突研究超越孤立的转变分析，为理解暴力的生命周期提供了一个框架，揭示了冲突轨迹的空间相互依赖性模式。

Abstract: Existing models of political violence often emphasize discrete transitions, when conflicts emerge, escalate, or subside, without considering the longer trajectories of violence that accumulate across time and space. This paper introduces a spatially explicit longitudinal sequence analysis to address this gap. Using event-level data from the Armed Conflict Location and Event Dataset covering Africa from 1997 to 2024, we classify locations according to the intensity and spatial concentration of violence, tracing how these states evolve into distinct conflict trajectories. Applying optimal matching and clustering techniques, we identify six recurrent patterns ranging from short-lived, localized outbreaks to protracted high-intensity conflicts. We further assess how these trajectories align across neighboring areas, revealing evidence of spatial interdependence, particularly in border regions. By highlighting the temporal rhythms and geographic linkages of political violence, the study advances conflict research beyond isolated transitions and provides a framework for understanding the life cycles of violence.

</details>

### [239] [CrossCheck: Input Validation for WAN Control Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05792)
*Alexander Krentsel,Rishabh Iyer,Isaac Keslassy,Bharath Modhipalli,Sylvia Ratnasamy,Anees Shaikh,Rob Shakir*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: CrossCheck是一个SDN控制器输入验证系统，通过检测错误输入预防网络中断，在生产环境中验证有效且误报率低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模WAN运营商的分析表明，无效输入是导致重大网络中断的主要原因，需要一种能够提前检测并预防这些问题的系统。

Method: 开发了CrossCheck系统，作为SDN控制器的影子验证系统，在生产WAN中部署四周进行验证，同时通过模拟测试检测各种无效输入场景。

Result: 在生产部署中准确检测到唯一一次无效输入事件，误报率为0%；模拟测试显示能可靠检测小至5%的需求扰动（100%准确率），在高达30%的遥测数据损坏情况下仍保持接近零的误报率。

Conclusion: CrossCheck能有效预防由SDN控制基础设施错误输入导致的网络中断，在实际生产环境中验证可行，对运营商负担小，具有实用价值。

Abstract: We present CrossCheck, a system that validates inputs to the Software-Defined Networking (SDN) controller in a Wide Area Network (WAN). By detecting incorrect inputs - often stemming from bugs in the SDN control infrastructure - CrossCheck alerts operators before they trigger network outages.
  Our analysis at a large-scale WAN operator identifies invalid inputs as a leading cause of major outages, and we show how CrossCheck would have prevented those incidents. We deployed CrossCheck as a shadow validation system for four weeks in a production WAN, during which it accurately detected the single incident of invalid inputs that occurred while sustaining a 0% false positive rate under normal operation, hence imposing little additional burden on operators. In addition, we show through simulation that CrossCheck reliably detects a wide range of invalid inputs (e.g., detecting demand perturbations as small as 5% with 100% accuracy) and maintains a near-zero false positive rate for realistic levels of noisy, missing, or buggy telemetry data (e.g., sustaining zero false positives with up to 30% of corrupted telemetry data).

</details>


### [240] [A Dual-AoI-based Approach for Optimal Transmission Scheduling in Wireless Monitoring Systems with Random Data Arrivals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06042)
*Yuchong Zhang,Yi Cao,Xianghui Cao*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文针对物联网无线监控系统中的信息新鲜度调度问题，提出了一种双AoI模型和基于MDP的低复杂度调度策略，有效解决了异步AoI演化带来的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物联网系统中实时监控和决策对信息新鲜度要求高，但有限信道资源、数据到达随机性和无线信道不可靠性制约了信息新鲜度（AoI）。传统调度策略仅依赖监控中心的AoI，无法有效处理本地传感器与监控中心之间的异步AoI演化问题。

Method: 提出双AoI模型捕捉异步AoI动态，将问题建模为最小化长期时间平均AoI函数。基于马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）开发调度策略，分析确定性平稳最优策略的存在性和单调性。推导出具有信道状态依赖阈值结构的低复杂度调度策略，并建立AoI目标稳定性的充要条件。

Result: 仿真结果表明，所提出的调度策略优于现有方法。该策略能够有效处理异步AoI演化，在有限信道资源下实现更好的信息新鲜度性能。

Conclusion: 双AoI模型和基于MDP的低复杂度调度策略能够有效解决无线监控系统中的信息新鲜度调度问题，为物联网实时监控系统提供了理论依据和实用解决方案。

Abstract: In Internet of Things (IoTs), the freshness of system status information is crucial for real-time monitoring and decision-making. This paper studies the transmission scheduling problem in wireless monitoring systems, where information freshness -- typically quantified by the Age of Information (AoI) -- is heavily constrained by limited channel resources and influenced by factors such as the randomness of data arrivals and unreliable wireless channel. Such randomness leads to asynchronous AoI evolution at local sensors and the monitoring center, rendering conventional scheduling policies that rely solely on the monitoring center's AoI inefficient. To this end, we propose a dual-AoI model that captures asynchronous AoI dynamics and formulate the problem as minimizing a long-term time-average AoI function. We develop a scheduling policy based on Markov decision process (MDP) to solve the problem, and analyze the existence and monotonicity of a deterministic stationary optimal policy. Moreover, we derive a low-complexity scheduling policy which exhibits a channel-state-dependent threshold structure. In addition, we establish a necessary and sufficient condition for the stability of the AoI objective. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed policy outperforms existing approaches.

</details>
